Result: 在Mind2Web Hard上达到89.47%成功率，排名第三，大幅领先其他开源基线。

Conclusion: 性能提升源于整个系统中认知契约的一致应用，而非单一技巧。

中文摘要：我们提出了SUPERBROWSER，一个自主网页导航代理，其设计基于一个单一的指导假设：网页代理应该像人一样浏览。人类在阅读页面时并不会保留他们看到的每一个像素；他们会查看几个候选目标，决定一个，并只记住保持目标所需的信息。我们将这种感知-认知-行动三元组作为三个耦合机制进行操作化。首先，一个视觉优先的边界框管道在每个截图上标记候选交互区域，并异步预取给语言模型，使得“眼睛”先于“手”。其次，一个三角色大脑——一个负责分类和路由的编排器、一个每隔几步评估进展的规划器，以及一个发出每步动作的工作者——将战略推理与操作推理分离。第三，一个结构化的账本只存储一个人会存储的内容：目标、最近三个动作、一小组事实和死胡同，以及少量检查点；一个六阶段驱逐循环系统地丢弃实时上下文中的过时截图、状态块和推理痕迹。动作执行是一个三层点击级联（Chrome DevTools协议到Puppeteer到脚本化），具有人性化的贝塞尔运动，以及一个识别chevron的边界框捕捉器，解决了“大标签旁边的小箭头”歧义问题。在Mind2Web Hard基准测试（66个任务）上，SUPERBROWSER达到了89.47%的成功率，总体排名第三，并且以较大优势领先于所有已发布的开源/研究浏览器代理基线。我们认为，这种改进并非来自任何单一技巧，而是来自整个系统中认知契约的一致应用。

Original abstract: We present SUPERBROWSER, an autonomous web-navigation agent designed against a single guiding hypothesis: a web agent should browse the way a person browses. A human reading a page does not retain every pixel they have seen; they look at a few candidate targets, decide on one, and remember only what is needed to keep the goal alive. We operationalize this perception-cognition-action triad as three coupled mechanisms. First, a vision-first bounding-box pipeline labels candidate interactive regions on every screenshot and feeds them, asynchronously prefetched, to the language model so that the "eye" precedes the "hand". Second, a three-role brain -- an Orchestrator that classifies and routes, a Planner that evaluates progress every few steps, and a Worker that emits per-step actions -- separates strategic from operational reasoning. Third, a structured Ledger stores only what a person would: the goal, the last three actions, a small set of facts and dead-ends, and a handful of checkpoints; a six-phase eviction loop systematically discards stale screenshots, state blobs, and reasoning traces from the live context. Action execution is a three-tier click cascade (Chrome DevTools Protocol to Puppeteer to scripted) with humanized Bezier motion, plus a chevron-aware bounding-box snapper that resolves the "small arrow beside a large label" ambiguity. On the Mind2Web Hard benchmark (66 tasks), SUPERBROWSER attains 89.47% success, placing third overall and ahead of every published open/research browser-agent baseline by a large margin. We argue that the gain comes not from any single trick but from the consistent application of a cognitive contract throughout the system.

</details>


### [31] [Capacity, Not Format: Rethinking Structured Reasoning Failures](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09410v1)
*Hengxin Fan*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究结构化输出对推理的影响，发现容量竞争机制，对agent格式化输出设计有直接启发。

TL;DR: 结构化输出的成本取决于模型空闲容量；容量不足时，格式化通过截断和纯容量竞争两种机制导致性能下降；先推理后格式化可缓解该问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作将结构化输出视为统一的推理税，但忽略了模型容量差异；本文旨在分离格式化成本与提示长度混淆，揭示容量依赖的退化机制。

Method: 使用信息匹配的散文控制和四级模式复杂度梯度，在4个模型和5个基准测试中比较JSON与CoT格式，控制token预算和截断，并设计延迟结构消融实验。

Result: 容量充足的模型（如Sonnet）无退化；容量受限模型（如Haiku、GPT-4o-mini）因截断或纯容量竞争显著下降（降幅达36.2pp和28.0pp）；格式惩罚随模式复杂度增加；前沿模型（Opus 4.7）在复杂任务上下降约5.3pp；延迟结构消融恢复大部分准确率。

Conclusion: 结构化输出不应被普遍避免，而应匹配模型容量；当模型接近极限时，应优先推理后格式化，以减少容量竞争带来的性能损失。

中文摘要：先前的工作将结构化输出视为一种推理税，但这种框架是不完整的：格式化的成本在很大程度上取决于模型的空闲容量。使用信息匹配的散文控制和一个四级模式复杂度梯度，我们在4个模型和5个基准测试中分离了格式特定效应与提示长度混淆，在成功生成的响应中实现了0%的解析失败。我们发现结构化格式是容量依赖的。具有足够余量的模型吸收JSON约束而不退化（Sonnet: MATH-Hard上JSON 88.7±4.0% vs CoT 89.3±1.7%）。相反，格式严重退化接近其极限的模型，通过两种不同的机制。首先，在标准token预算下，Haiku下降了36.2个百分点（p < 0.0001），主要是由于截断。其次，即使在消除截断的扩展预算下，GPT-4o-mini下降了28.0个百分点（p < 0.001），揭示了独立于token耗尽的纯容量竞争。这种格式惩罚随模式复杂度增加（McNemar p < 0.0001），且不能仅由提示长度解释。此外，这些结果对前沿模型免疫性的说法提出了质疑：在AIME竞赛数学中，Opus 4.7在JSON下从96.2%下降到91.0%（-5.3个百分点；显示的百分比独立取整，精确差异为7/133 = 5.26pp ≈ 5.3pp）。一种延迟结构消融——在格式化前自由推理——恢复了大部分丢失的准确率（3次运行平均：80-87%），支持容量竞争机制。实际意义不是避免结构化输出，而是使其与容量匹配：当模型接近其极限时，先思考，后格式化。

Original abstract: Prior work treats structured output as a reasoning tax, but this framing is incomplete: the cost of formatting depends strongly on a model's spare capacity. Using information-matched prose controls and a four-level schema complexity gradient, we separate format-specific effects from prompt-length confounds across 4 models and 5 benchmarks with 0% parse failures on successfully generated responses.
  We find that structured formats are capacity-dependent. Models with sufficient headroom absorb JSON constraints without degradation (Sonnet: $88.7\pm4.0$% JSON vs. $89.3\pm1.7$% CoT on MATH-Hard). In contrast, formats severely degrade models operating near their limits through two distinct mechanisms. First, under standard token budgets, Haiku drops 36.2pp ($p < 0.0001$) largely due to truncation. Second, even with extended budgets eliminating truncation, GPT-4o-mini drops 28.0pp ($p < 0.001$), revealing pure capacity competition independent of token exhaustion.
  This format penalty scales with schema complexity (McNemar $p < 0.0001$) and cannot be explained by prompt length alone. Furthermore, these results qualify claims of frontier model immunity: on AIME competition math, Opus 4.7 drops from 96.2% to 91.0% under JSON ($-5.3$pp; the displayed percentages are independently rounded, exact difference is $7/133 = 5.26$pp $\approx 5.3$pp). A delayed-structure ablation -- reasoning freely before formatting -- recovers most of the lost accuracy (3-run mean: 80--87%), supporting the capacity competition mechanism. The practical implication is not to avoid structured output, but to match it to capacity: when a model is near its limits, think first, format later.

</details>


### [32] [WeaveBench: A Long-Horizon, Real-World Benchmark for Computer-Use Agents with Hybrid Interfaces](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09426v3)
*Wanli Li,Bowen Zhou,Yunyao Yu,Zhou Xu,Yifan Yang,Dongsheng Li,Caihua Shan*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 长期混合界面computer-use agent基准，对agent评测有直接价值。

TL;DR: WeaveBench是一个长期混合接口基准测试，要求代理结合GUI和CLI/代码操作，最佳通过率仅41.2%，轨迹感知法官显示结果评分高估性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准将GUI、CLI、代码等接口作为分离能力评估，缺乏对长期跨接口编排的测试。

Method: 构建114个跨8个领域的真实任务，代理需在单次轨迹中组合GUI与CLI/代码操作，并引入轨迹感知法官检测捷径行为。

Result: 最佳通过率41.2%，轨迹感知法官显示结果评分高估实际性能。

Conclusion: WeaveBench揭示了CUA评估的关键差距，为衡量代理协调多接口能力提供了有效测试平台。

中文摘要：计算机使用代理（CUA）越来越多地在结合可视化桌面控制、命令行执行、代码编辑、浏览器和外部工具的运行环境中运行。然而，现有基准测试通常将这些接口作为可分离的能力进行评估，导致长期跨接口编排的测试不足。因此，我们引入了WeaveBench，这是一个长期混合接口基准测试，包含来自8个真实世界工作领域的114个任务，基于真实用户请求和可公开验证的工件。每个任务要求代理在单个轨迹中结合GUI观察/操作与CLI/代码操作。我们在部署了CLI代理运行时的真实Ubuntu桌面上评估这些任务，并辅以一个最小的桌面控制插件。我们还提出了一个配套的轨迹感知法官，它检查交付物、文件、截图、日志和操作痕迹，同时检测捷径行为，例如伪造的视觉证据或硬编码的指标。在顶级模型-运行时配对中，最佳通过率仅达到41.2%，表明该基准测试远未饱和。轨迹感知法官进一步揭示，仅基于结果的评分会大大高估代理性能。总体而言，WeaveBench暴露了CUA评估中的关键差距，并提供了一个有效的测试平台来衡量代理是否能够在长期真实世界任务中协调GUI、CLI和代码操作。

Original abstract: Computer-use agents (CUAs) increasingly operate in runtimes that combine visual desktop control, command-line execution, code editing, browsers, and external tools. Existing benchmarks, however, often evaluate these interfaces as separable capabilities, leaving long-horizon cross-interface orchestration under-tested. Thus, we introduce WeaveBench, a long-horizon hybrid-interface benchmark with 114 tasks across 8 real-world work domains, grounded in real user requests and publicly verifiable artifacts. Each task requires agents to combine GUI observations/actions with CLI/code operations within a single trajectory. We evaluate these tasks on a real Ubuntu desktop inside deployed CLI-agent runtimes, augmented with a minimal desktop-control plugin. We also propose a companion trajectory-aware judge that inspects deliverables, files, screenshots, logs, and action traces, while detecting shortcut behaviors such as fabricated visual evidence or hard-coded metrics. Across frontier model-runtime pairings, the best PassRate reaches only 41.2%, showing the benchmark remains far from saturated. The trajectory-aware judge further reveals that outcome-only grading substantially overestimates agent performance. Overall, WeaveBench exposes a critical gap in CUA evaluation and provides an effective testbed to measure whether agents can orchestrate GUI, CLI, and code operations across long-horizon real-world tasks.

### [33] [Bayesian Selective Latent Inference for Wastewater-First Influenza Monitoring](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09433v1)
*Yixuan Zhang,Yang Song,Hao Wang,Samir Bhatt,Hengguan Huang*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有废水模型假设固定证据集，而通用方法将官方监测视为可互换的昂贵特征，未能充分利用废水优先的决策灵活性。

Method: 将废水优先监测建模为选择性决策问题，提出BSLI方法，包括贝叶斯后验维护、科学门控可回答性认证和成本校准贝尔曼策略。

Result: 在包含5,933个预测回合和3,102个源模糊性回合的基准上，BSLI改善了匹配预算的成本-性能前沿，并保留了保守弃权。

中文摘要：废水流感监测可以在临床报告之前揭示社区传播，但仅凭废水本身并不能完全作为人类负担的可识别代理。现有的废水模型假设一个固定的证据集，而通用的证据获取方法则将官方监测流视为可互换的昂贵特征。我们将以废水为先的流感监测视为一个选择性决策问题：从强制性的废水证据开始，系统必须决定废水是否足够，接下来查询哪个延迟的官方流，以及在源模糊性下何时弃权是唯一科学上可辩护的行动。我们提出了贝叶斯选择性潜在推理（BSLI），这是一种原则性的贝叶斯方法，它维护关于潜在负担和可识别性的后验，通过明确的科学门控来认证可回答性，并利用精确的成本校准贝尔曼策略优化查询停止决策。我们证明了关键的变分、可回答性、贝尔曼最优性和一维成本校准性质。在一个包含5,933个预测回合和3,102个源模糊性回合的固定公共数据基准上，BSLI改善了匹配预算的成本-性能前沿，同时在源模糊性下保留了保守的弃权。

Original abstract: Wastewater influenza surveillance can reveal community circulation before clinical reporting, but wastewater alone is not a fully identifiable proxy for human burden. Existing wastewater models assume a fixed evidence set, while generic evidence-acquisition methods treat official surveillance streams as interchangeable costly features. We cast wastewater-first influenza monitoring as a selective decision problem: starting from mandatory wastewater evidence, the system must decide whether wastewater is sufficient, which delayed official stream to query next, and when abstention is the only scientifically defensible action under source ambiguity. We propose Bayesian Selective Latent Inference (BSLI), a principled Bayesian method that maintains a posterior over latent burden and identifiability, certifies answerability through explicit scientific gates, and optimizes query-stop decisions with an exact cost-calibrated Bellman policy. We prove the key variational, answerability, Bellman-optimality, and one-dimensional cost-calibration properties. On a fixed public-data benchmark with 5,933 forecasting episodes and 3,102 source-ambiguity episodes, BSLI improves the matched-budget cost-performance frontier while preserving conservative abstention under source ambiguity.

### [34] [AliyunConsoleAgent: Training Web Agents in Real-World Cloud Environments via Distillation and Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09447v1)
*Bojie Rong,Zheyu Shen,Qiaoping Wang,Pengfei Kang,Yang Xu,Yawen Wei,Hanyu Wu,Zhi Zhao,Leihao Pei,Linquan Jiang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 两阶段训练：首先在蒸馏的前沿模型轨迹上进行监督微调（SFT），然后使用组相对策略优化（GRPO）和双通道结果奖励模型在真实云环境中进行强化学习。同时构建基于Terraform和LLM的高确定性推出系统以隔离环境噪声，并引入基于后端审计日志的规则化奖励评估协议。

Conclusion: 该框架有效实现了从指令跟随到自主决策的进化，为大规模云文档验证提供了低成本、高隐私的可行方案，显著缩小了与前沿模型的性能差距。

中文摘要：我们提出了AliyunConsoleAgent，一个用于真实云控制台自动化文档验证的web智能体框架。主流云平台包含数百个产品，且功能迭代迅速，导致控制台UI常常与对应的文档产生偏差。验证文档描述的流程是否准确反映当前控制台并可以端到端执行，每年需要约400万次重复检查，而人工覆盖率仍低于1%。尽管基于前沿专有模型的智能体系统取得了较高的成功率，但其高昂的成本和数据隐私限制阻碍了大规模部署。我们提出了一种两阶段训练范式：在蒸馏的前沿模型轨迹上进行监督微调（SFT），然后使用组相对策略优化（GRPO）和真实云环境中的双通道结果奖励模型进行强化学习。为了支持大规模RL训练，我们构建了一个高确定性的推出系统，采用基于Terraform的资源预置和LLM驱动的按需置备，有效地从训练信号中隔离环境噪声。我们进一步引入了一种基于后端审计日志的规则化奖励评估协议，提供客观、抗奖励破解的结果判断。我们的模型从机械性的指令跟随演变为自主决策，具备云控制台和产品特定的理解能力。在一个具有挑战性的278任务基准测试中（最佳前沿模型仅达到65.34%），AliyunConsoleAgent-32B实现了63.52%的平均成功率——相比基础模型提升了20.24个百分点，与最佳前沿专有模型差距缩小到1.82个百分点（bootstrap 95%置信区间[-1.27, 7.39]），同时推理成本降低了92%。

Original abstract: We present AliyunConsoleAgent, a web agent framework for automated documentation verification in real-world cloud consoles. Major cloud platforms encompass hundreds of products with rapid feature iteration, causing console UIs to frequently diverge from their corresponding documentation. Verifying that documented procedures accurately reflect the current console and can be executed end-to-end demands an estimated 4 million recurring inspections annually, yet manual coverage remains below 1%. While agent systems built on frontier proprietary models achieve high success rates, their prohibitive cost and data privacy constraints preclude large-scale deployment. We propose a two-stage training paradigm: supervised fine-tuning (SFT) on distilled frontier-model trajectories, followed by reinforcement learning using Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) and a dual-channel outcome reward model in real cloud environments. To support large-scale RL training, we construct a high-determinism rollout system featuring Terraform-based resource pre-provisioning and LLM-driven on-demand provisioning, which effectively isolates environment noise from the training signal. We further introduce a rule-based reward evaluation protocol grounded in backend audit logs, providing objective, reward-hacking-resistant outcome judgment. Our model evolves from mechanical instruction following to autonomous decision-making with cloud console and product-specific understanding. Experiments on a challenging 278-task benchmark where the best frontier model achieves only 65.34% demonstrate that AliyunConsoleAgent-32B achieves a 63.52% mean success rate -- a 20.24 percentage-point improvement over the base model, narrowing the gap to the best frontier proprietary model to 1.82 pp (bootstrap 95% CI [-1.27, 7.39]) -- at 92% lower inference cost.

### [35] [Deterministic Integrity Gates for LLM-Assisted Clinical Manuscript Preparation: An Auditable Biomedical Informatics Architecture](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09500v4)
*Yoojin Nam,Jinhoon Jeong,Namkug Kim*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出确定性验证架构用于LLM生成，对agent验证可审计性有启发。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM生成文本流畅但易含伪造引用、数字错误和报告指南缺失，现有工具不验证，自批评继承盲点，需要可靠的验证方法。

Method: 设计三原则架构：分解工作流、阶段门控、最便宜机制；构建完整性门控分类法，优先确定性检查；实现MedSci Skills工具包（43技能，21确定性检测器）。

Result: 在STARD、PRISMA、STROBE管道中内容哈希均干净，门控暴露真实缺陷；对27个注入缺陷，确定性门控全部检测且无假阳性，而LLM审查仅检测11个。

Conclusion: 尽可能确定性的验证提供可审计、可重执行的证据，用于人类检查LLM稿件，不声称达到人类水平但支持可行性验证。

中文摘要：随着自主研究代理和AI联合科学家系统推动大型语言模型（LLM）从起草转向端到端稿件生产，瓶颈从生成转向验证。流畅的LLM输出可能隐藏伪造的引用、偏离源表格的数字以及未满足的报告指南条目；现有工具在生成时不进行验证，而自我批评继承了产生自信伪造的盲点。我们描述了一种将生成与验证配对的架构，基于三个原则：将工作流程分解为自包含的技能，用失败即停止的门控每个阶段转换，用最便宜的足够机制解决每个完整性问题——在确定性可重执行检查足够时使用它，仅在不可避免时才使用散文级别的探针。这种尽可能确定性的拆分，组织成一个完整性门控分类法，是核心贡献。它被实现为MedSci Skills，一个包含43个技能的开源工具包，其中有一个21个检测器的确定性层，在三个公共数据集管道（STARD、PRISMA、STROBE）和种子缺陷消融实验中进行了评估。在三个管道中，每个内容哈希清单都验证为干净，门控暴露了真实缺陷；在27个相同的注入缺陷中，确定性门控检测到全部27个，且在匹配的干净夹具上无假阳性，而单提示LLM审查员检测到11个，其遗漏在于代码、参考文献和样式缺陷——这些是散文所隐藏的。尽可能确定性的验证产生了一个可审计、可重执行的轨迹，暴露了人类检查LLM辅助稿件所需的证据：可行性和可重复性证据，而非人类竞争力质量的声明，后者由一项单独的盲法研究处理。MedSci Skills采用MIT许可并已归档（v3.8.0）。

Original abstract: As autonomous research agents and AI co-scientist systems push large language models (LLMs) from drafting toward end-to-end manuscript production, the bottleneck shifts from generation to verification. Fluent LLM output can hide fabricated citations, numbers that drift from source tables, and unmet reporting-guideline items; existing tools generate without verifying, and self-critique inherits the blind spots that produce confident fabrication. We describe an architecture pairing generation with verification, resting on three principles: decompose the workflow into self-contained skills, gate every stage transition with halt-on-failure, and resolve each integrity question with the cheapest sufficient mechanism, a deterministic, re-executable check where one suffices and a prose-level probe only where interpretation is unavoidable. This determinism-where-possible split, organized as an integrity-gate taxonomy, is the core contribution. It is realized as MedSci Skills, an open-source toolkit of 43 skills with a 21-detector deterministic tier, evaluated on three public-dataset pipelines (STARD, PRISMA, STROBE) and a seeded-defect ablation. Across the three pipelines every content-hash manifest verified clean and the gates surfaced real defects; on 27 identical injected defects the deterministic gates detected all 27 with no false positives on the matched clean fixtures, whereas a single-prompt LLM reviewer detected 11, its misses in code, bibliography, and style defects the prose hides. Determinism-where-possible verification yields an auditable, re-executable trail that exposes the evidence a human needs to check an LLM-assisted manuscript: feasibility and reproducibility evidence, not a claim of human-competitive quality, which a separate blinded study addresses. MedSci Skills is MIT-licensed and archived (v3.8.0).

</details>


### [36] [AI Scientists Are Only as Good as Their Evidence: A Stratified Ablation of Proprietary Data and Reasoning Skills in Drug-Asset Valuation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09556v1)
*Yinan Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究AI Scientist agent的证据依赖，对agent评估有迁移价值。

TL;DR: 在药物资产估值任务中，专有证据语料库（C）显著提升了AI科学家的决策质量，而仅改进推理框架（B）无法突破事实覆盖度的上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI科学家评估通常聚焦模型和推理，但本文假设知识密集型决策的限制因素是证据访问。

Method: 在估值智能体上进行三组消融：A（仅网页LLM）、B（增加公共工具、剧本和审计）、C（增加专有语料库），在13个资产上比较校准、覆盖度和决策质量。

Result: C在黄金覆盖度（0.96 vs 0.25/0.38）和完整性感知决策效用（7.43 vs 1.76/2.57）上远超A和B；B仅改善校准但未提升事实上限。

Conclusion: 推理框架重要但非关键；专有证据设定了AI科学家知识的上界，从而决定决策质量。

中文摘要：AI Scientist智能体通常被评估时，仿佛能力主要取决于模型质量、提示或推理框架。我们在药物资产估值中测试了一个不同的假设：对于知识密集型科学决策，限制因素往往是智能体能够访问的证据基础。我们在一个生产级估值智能体上进行了受控的三组消融实验：A是仅使用网络的普通LLM分析师，B增加了公共结构化工具以及14维度估值剧本、验证器、客观性策略和红队，C增加了专有的Noah AI语料库，包含精选的管线、试验和交易情报。在13个资产的分层基准上，B改进了校准和审计纪律：区间内准确率从0.80提高到0.89，客观性从3.16提高到3.30。但B并未消除事实上限。在能力超集核算下，A和B仅恢复了精选黄金竞争记录的0.25和0.38，而C恢复了0.96；在精选长尾子集上，C达到0.93，而A/B为0.26/0.30。原始盲审决策质量A和B相似（7.01 vs 6.96），因此我们引入了完整性感知决策效用：知情决策质量 = 决策质量 × 黄金覆盖度。在此指标下，C达到7.43，而A/B为1.76/2.57。即使完美的非专有数据报告，在B的覆盖度下上限也仅为3.83。结果并非推理框架不重要；它们改善了校准和纪律。相反，专有证据设定了AI科学家所能知道并因此做出决策的上限。

Original abstract: AI Scientist agents are often evaluated as if capability were mainly a function of model quality, prompting, or reasoning scaffolds. We test a different hypothesis in drug-asset valuation: for knowledge-intensive scientific decisions, the limiting factor is often the evidence substrate the agent can access. We run a controlled three-arm ablation on a production valuation agent: A is a plain web-only LLM analyst, B adds public structured tools plus a 14-dimension valuation playbook, verifier, objectivity policy and red-team, and C adds the proprietary Noah AI corpus of curated pipeline, trial and deal intelligence. Across a 13-asset stratified benchmark, B improves calibration and audit discipline: tier-in-range accuracy rises from 0.80 to 0.89 and objectivity from 3.16 to 3.30. But B does not remove the factual ceiling. Under capability-superset accounting, A and B recover only 0.25 and 0.38 of the curated gold competitive record, while C recovers 0.96; on the curated long-tail subset, C reaches 0.93 vs. 0.26/0.30. Raw blind-panel decision quality is similar for A and B (7.01 vs. 6.96), so we introduce completeness-aware decision utility: informed decision-quality = decision-quality x gold-coverage. On this metric, C reaches 7.43 vs. 1.76/2.57 for A/B. Even a perfect non-proprietary-data report would be capped at 3.83 by B's coverage. The result is not that reasoning scaffolds are unimportant; they improve calibration and discipline. Rather, proprietary evidence sets the upper bound of what the AI Scientist can know and therefore decide.

### [37] [PRISM: Recovering Instruction Sets from Language Model Activations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09563v1)
*Gilad Gressel,Rahul Pankajakshan,Julia Diament,Efim Hudis,Krishnashree Achuthan,Yisroel Mirsky*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 从LLM激活恢复指令集，直接用于agent监控与安全。

TL;DR: PRISM是一种从LLM隐藏状态中解码活跃指令集的方法，通过法官引导的GRPO训练，在多种场景下优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法无法在代理设置中恢复完整的指令集，包括子目标、约束、提示注入等，需要更好的监控方法。

Method: 提出PRISM，一个激活条件解释器，使用法官引导的GRPO训练，直接从隐藏状态解码出活跃指令的项目符号列表。

Result: 在良性、约束、提示注入和隐藏目标设置中，PRISM优于激活到语言基线，尤其在安全相关目标上表现突出。

Conclusion: PRISM有效解决了指令集检索问题，为LLM代理监控提供了可靠的方法。

中文摘要：随着LLMs被部署为代理，可靠的监控需要不仅知道它们的输出，还要知道哪些指令正在引导它们的行为。当模型推断出非预期的子目标、遵循上下文线索、或受到提示注入和隐藏目标的影响时，这变得困难。虽然激活到语言方法表明隐藏状态可以揭示自然语言信息，但现有方法并非旨在恢复在代理设置中同时活跃的完整指令、约束、禁止和子目标集。我们将此问题形式化为指令集检索，并引入PRISM，一个激活条件解释器，它将冻结目标模型的隐藏状态解码为活跃指令的忠实项目符号列表。与之前的激活到语言方法不同，PRISM直接训练以恢复指令集，使用法官引导的GRPO来奖励被覆盖的指令并惩罚不受支持的指令。在良性、约束、提示注入和隐藏目标设置中，PRISM优于激活到语言基线，特别是在安全相关的目标上。

Original abstract: As LLMs are deployed as agents, reliable monitoring requires knowing not only what they output, but which instructions are steering their behavior. This is difficult when models infer unintended subgoals, follow contextual cues, or are influenced by prompt injections and hidden objectives. While activation-to-language methods suggest that hidden states can reveal natural-language information, existing approaches are not designed to recover the full set of simultaneous instructions, constraints, prohibitions, and subgoals active in agentic settings. We formalize this problem as instruction set retrieval and introduce PRISM, an activation-conditioned interpreter that decodes hidden states from a frozen target model into a faithful bullet list of active instructions. Unlike prior activation-to-language methods, PRISM is trained to recover instruction sets directly, using judge-guided GRPO to reward covered instructions and penalize unsupported ones. Across benign, constrained, prompt-injection, and hidden-objective settings, PRISM outperforms activation-to-language baselines, especially on security-relevant objectives.

### [38] [Self-Explainability in Self-Adaptive and Self-Organising Systems: Status and Research Directions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09568v1)
*Tom Beyer,Svea Wisy,Sven Tomforde*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 自我解释性综述，对agent可解释性有参考价值。

TL;DR: 本文对自解释性（SX）进行了系统文献综述，提出了统一定义、分类法和自解释性级别，发现大多数SX方法仍停留在概念阶段，缺乏实际实现和标准化评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自适应和自组织系统的复杂性增加，使其难以理解和信任，而现有可解释AI（XAI）旨在解释AI决策，但更高级的目标是系统自我解释（SX），因此需要系统化梳理SX研究现状以指导未来工作。

Method: 采用系统文献综述方法，分析现有SX方法及其领域、目标和评估方式，进而提出统一定义、分类法和自解释性级别框架。

Result: 大多数SX方法为概念性，缺乏实际实现；目前尚无正式或事实上的SX评估标准，存在显著研究空白。

中文摘要：由人工智能（AI）进步推动的自适应和自组织系统的日益复杂性，使它们变得越来越难以理解和信任。虽然可解释人工智能旨在提供对AI决策的洞察，但一个更高级的目标是让系统能够自我解释——这种能力被称为自解释性（SX）。本文对SX进行了系统文献综述，分析了现有方法，包括其领域、目标和评估方法。该综述提出了SX的统一定义和分类法，并引入了自解释性级别，为定位当前和未来研究提供了一个框架。我们的结果表明，大多数SX方法仍然是概念性的，很少有实际实现。此外，目前没有正式或事实上的标准来评估SX，突出了一个主要的研究空白。因此，这项工作为在复杂系统中推进自解释性建立了基础和路线图。

Original abstract: The growing complexity of self-adaptive and self-organising systems, fuelled by advances in Artificial Intelligence (AI), has made them increasingly difficult to understand and trust. While Explainable AI aims to provide insight into AI decision-making, a more advanced goal is for systems to explain themselves - an ability referred to as Self-Explainability (SX). This article presents a systematic literature review on SX, analysing existing approaches, including their domains, targets, and evaluation methods. The review develops a unified definition and taxonomy of SX and introduces Levels of Self-Explainability, providing a framework for positioning current and future research. Our results show that most SX approaches remain conceptual, with few practical implementations. Moreover, there is currently no formal or de facto standard for evaluating SX, highlighting a major research gap. This work thus establishes a foundation and roadmap for advancing Self-Explainability in complex systems.

### [39] [From 0-to-1 to 1-to-N: Reproducible Engineering Evidence for MetaAI Recursive Self-Design](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09663v1)
*Dun Li,Jiatao Li,Hongzhi Li*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了系统化地定义和评估递归自设计（AI辅助修改自身构建过程）这一新兴范式，提出一个可操作的证据框架。

Method: 定义四个操作化标准（可检查目标系统、元级修改器、反馈导向选择、递归延续），并映射现有公共系统（DGM、STOP、Goedel Agent、ShinkaEvolve），同时提供MetaAI-Mini协议和代码库。

Original abstract: Recursive self-design refers to AI-assisted modification of the mechanisms by which an AI system is built, evaluated, and improved. This paper treats MetaAI not as a mature paradigm, but as a working term for a human-seeded, AI-expanded development pattern in which the design space itself becomes a target of modification. We propose an operational evidence framework with four criteria: inspectable target system, meta-level modifier, feedback-directed selection, and recursive continuation. We then map public systems, including Darwin Goedel Machine (DGM), STOP, Goedel Agent, and ShinkaEvolve, against these criteria. DGM provides the most direct currently reported evidence: its published results show improvement from 20% to 50% on SWE-bench Verified and from 14.2% to 30.7% on full Polyglot after 80 iterations, with ablations suggesting that both open-ended exploration and self-improvement contribute. Finally, we provide MetaAI-Mini, a reproducible HumanEval-based protocol and codebase. Because no completed model run is included in this build, MetaAI-Mini is reported as a protocol rather than as an experimental result.

### [40] [SpatialWorld: Benchmarking Interactive Spatial Reasoning of Multimodal Agents in Real-World Tasks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09669v2)
*Hongcheng Gao,Hailong Qu,Jingyi Tang,Jiahao Wang,Zihao Huang,Hengkang Qiao,Shihong Huang,Junming Yang,Yi Li,Hongyixuan Yuan,Wenjie Li,Bohan Zeng,Wenbo Li,Bo Wang,Jianhui Liu,Olive Huang,Haoyang Huang,Wentao Zhang,Guoqing Huang,Nan Duan,Yinpeng Dong*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多模态agent空间推理基准，评估主动探索与长程规划能力

TL;DR: SpatialWorld是一个统一基准，通过集成异构模拟器和760个任务评估多模态大语言模型的交互式空间理解，发现最强模型GPT-5成功率仅17.4%，揭示主动探索和长期规划的瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准局限于被动评估或模拟器特定流程，无法有效评估多模态代理在复杂现实任务中的通用交互式空间理解能力。

Method: 构建SpatialWorld基准，集成八个异构模拟后端，采用共享协议，包含760个人工标注任务；每个任务提供初始状态、参考轨迹和终端验证器；代理在部分可观测下主动收集视觉证据并通过文本动作接口决策。

Result: 评估15个代理，GPT-5平均TSR 17.4%，Qwen-3.5为14.1%；存在任务成功与执行效率不匹配及领域特异性差异。

Conclusion: SpatialWorld作为严格测试平台，揭示了当前模型在主动探索和长期规划方面的瓶颈，表明鲁棒空间任务解决仍是重大挑战。

中文摘要：空间推理是多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）感知和操作物理世界的基础能力。然而，现有基准主要依赖被动评估（例如静态VQA）或特定于模拟器的流程，未能评估通用的交互式空间理解。我们提出了SpatialWorld，一个统一的基准，专门用于评估多模态代理在复杂现实任务中的交互式空间理解。它集成了八个异构模拟后端，采用共享的、与模拟器无关的协议，包含760个人工标注的任务，涵盖多样领域（例如家务、旅行、社交协作）。代理必须在仅视觉的部分可观测性下解决任务，主动收集以自我为中心的视觉证据，并通过统一、基于文本的动作接口（原生适用于MLLMs）表达决策。为进行可靠评估，每个任务包括一个经过人工验证的初始状态、一个参考轨迹和一个终端状态验证器。对15个高级代理的评估表明，鲁棒的空间任务解决仍然具有挑战性：最强的模型GPT-5平均任务成功率（TSR）仅为17.4%，而领先的开源模型Qwen-3.5达到14.1%。进一步分析揭示了任务成功与执行效率之间的明显不匹配，以及显著的领域特定性能差异。这些在主动探索和长期规划方面的瓶颈将SpatialWorld定位为未来空间代理的严格测试平台。

Original abstract: Spatial reasoning is a foundational capability for multimodal large language models (MLLMs) to perceive and operate within the physical world. However, existing benchmarks predominantly rely on passive evaluation (e.g., static VQA) or simulator-specific pipelines, failing to assess general interactive spatial understanding. We introduce SpatialWorld, a unified benchmark designed specifically for evaluating the interactive spatial understanding of multimodal agents in complex real-world tasks. Integrating eight heterogeneous simulation backends under a shared, simulator-agnostic protocol, SpatialWorld features 760 human-annotated tasks across diverse domains (e.g., household routines, travel, social collaboration). Agents must solve tasks under vision-only partial observability, actively gathering egocentric visual evidence and expressing decisions via a unified, text-based action interface native to MLLMs. For reliable evaluation, each task includes a human-validated initial state, a reference trajectory, and a terminal-state verifier. Evaluating 15 advanced agents reveals that robust spatial task solving remains challenging: the strongest model, GPT-5, achieves an average task success rate (TSR) of only 17.4%, while the leading open-source model, Qwen-3.5, reaches 14.1%. Further analysis exposes a clear mismatch between task success and execution efficiency, alongside substantial domain-specific performance variations. These bottlenecks in active exploration and long-horizon planning position SpatialWorld as a rigorous testbed for future spatial agents.

### [41] [(Auto)formalization is supposed to be easy: Trellis process semantics for spelling out rigorous proofs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09674v1)
*Wesley Pegden*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: Trellis使用LLM agent进行自动形式化证明，其确定性工作流可迁移至coding agent

TL;DR: 提出Trellis系统，通过受严格性含义启发的工作流，利用LLM代理迭代精炼自然语言证明，实现Lean自动形式化，并以低预算和通用代理获得可靠结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数学家认为严格证明意味着能够详细阐述证明的任何部分，这一观念启发我们设计自动形式化流程。

Method: 采用确定性约束的工作流，利用LLM代理通过迭代精炼自然语言证明来强制增量进展，过程语义确保严格性。

Result: 系统以适度预算和通用代理实现了可靠的自动形式化，并成功形式化了一个拉姆齐理论突破。

Conclusion: 自动形式化可以通过受严格性启发的流程而非专门训练来实现，证明了通用代理结合适当工作流的有效性。

中文摘要：我们提出Trellis：一个自动形式化系统，它利用LLM代理在确定性约束的工作流中，通过自然语言证明的迭代精炼，在Lean自动形式化任务中强制增量进展。我们的方法受到数学家关于什么是严格证明的常见观念的启发：即，能够例行公事地将证明的任何部分详细阐述。结果是一个系统，旨在以适度的预算和通用代理实现可靠的自动形式化，其针对自动形式化的专门化并非来自任何特定任务的代理训练，而是来自受严格性含义启发并由过程语义强制执行的工作流。我们提供了一个通过该过程生成的近期拉姆齐理论突破的端到端Lean形式化的链接。

Original abstract: We present Trellis: an autoformalization system that leverages LLM agents in a deterministically constrained workflow to enforce incremental progress in Lean autoformalization tasks through iterative refinement of natural language proofs. Our approach is motivated by the common mathematician's notion of what it means to have a rigorous proof in the first place: namely, that it would be routine to elaborate any part of the proof in further detail. The result is a system which aims to achieve reliable autoformalization on a modest budget and with generalist agents, with specialization to autoformalization coming not from any task-specific agent training but instead from a meaning-of-rigor inspired workflow enforced by process semantics. We link to an end-to-end Lean formalization of a recent Ramsey theory breakthrough produced by the process.

### [42] [Proxy Reward Internalization and Mechanistic Exploitation: A Learned Precursor to Reward Hacking and Its Generalization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09711v1)
*Mohammad Beigi,Ming Jin,Lifu Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 在代码RL环境中研究奖励黑客，对理解agent行为与评估有启发

TL;DR: PRIME是一种在奖励黑客变得可见之前出现的代理内化能力，可预测后续黑客行为的严重程度，并可作为对齐风险的早期预警信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究通常关注奖励黑客行为出现后的现象，但我们需要理解在可见失败之前代理RL学到了什么，以便提前预警。

Method: 在具有可被利用的pytest奖励的编码RL环境中，通过思维链监控、直接探测和激活级别概念向量测量PRIME，并分析其与后续黑客行为的关系。

Result: PRIME在持续奖励黑客之前阶段性出现，其直接探测评分可预测黑客的发作和严重程度；PRIME适应评估者变化，消融其激活可减少黑客；域内PRIME与域外不对齐相关。

Conclusion: 可被利用的代理RL放大了代理内化能力，PRIME可作为更广泛对齐风险的早期预警信号。

中文摘要：奖励黑客行为通常是在它变得可见后才被研究的，即当模型在未能完成预期任务的情况下获得高代理奖励时。我们转而研究代理强化学习在失败出现之前教会了模型什么。我们引入了代理奖励内化与机制性利用（PRIME），这是一种学习到的能力，用于评估任务正确性、预测代理接受度以及推理可被利用的代理-真实奖励差距。在具有可被利用的pytest奖励的编码强化学习环境中，我们通过思维链监控、直接探测和激活层级概念向量来测量PRIME。我们发现，PRIME在持续奖励黑客行为出现之前以阶段性顺序出现，并且其当前的直接探测评分可以预测后续黑客行为的开始时间和严重程度，即使当可见的黑客行为率仍然很低时也是如此。PRIME还能在评估者改变时适应，重新瞄准任何仍被奖励的代理-真实奖励差距，并在真实奖励抑制公开黑客行为时持续存在，且消融其激活方向可以减少黑客行为。在多个检查点上，域内PRIME追踪域外不对齐。这些结果共同表明，可被利用的代理强化学习放大了公开黑客行为上游的代理内化能力，使PRIME成为更广泛对齐风险的潜在早期预警信号。

Original abstract: Reward hacking is usually studied after it becomes visible, once a model earns high proxy reward while failing the intended task. We instead study what proxy RL teaches before that failure appears. We introduce Proxy Reward Internalization and Mechanistic Exploitation (PRIME), a learned capability to assess task correctness, predict proxy acceptance, and reason about exploitable proxy--gold gaps. In coding RL environments with exploitable pytest rewards, we measure PRIME through chain-of-thought monitoring, direct probes, and activation-level concept vectors. We find that PRIME emerges in a staged sequence before sustained reward hacking, and that its current direct-probe score forecasts later hack onset and severity even when the visible hack rate is still low. PRIME also adapts when the evaluator changes, retargeting to whichever proxy--gold gap remains rewarded and persisting when gold reward suppresses overt hacking, and ablating its activation directions reduces hacking. Across checkpoints, in-domain PRIME tracks out-of-domain misalignment. Together these results suggest that exploitable proxy RL amplifies a proxy-internalization capability upstream of visible hacking, making PRIME a candidate early-warning signal for broader alignment risk.

### [43] [SearchSwarm: Towards Delegation Intelligence in Agentic LLMs for Long-Horizon Deep Research](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09730v1)
*Pu Ning,Quan Chen,Kun Tao,Xinyu Tang,Tianshu Wang,Qianggang Cao,Xinyu Kong,Zujie Wen,Zhiqiang Zhang,Jun Zhou*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: SearchSwarm通过委派智能实现深度研究，其任务分解与委派方法可迁移至代码优化agent

TL;DR: 提出一种通过引导框架生成监督数据来训练模型获得任务分解与委托能力的方法，所得模型SearchSwarm-30B-A3B在长周期任务基准上取得领先结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长周期任务中上下文需求无限增长但模型上下文窗口有限，现有范式中主代理需具备委托智能，但缺乏训练数据且开源社区未探索如何合成数据训练该能力。

Method: 设计引导框架指导模型进行任务分解与委托，约束子代理返回适当结果；将引导生成轨迹作为监督微调数据，内化委托智能到模型权重中。

Result: SearchSwarm-30B-A3B在BrowseComp和BrowseComp-ZH上分别达到68.1和73.3，为同规模最佳。

Conclusion: 通过引导框架合成数据监督微调可有效赋予模型委托智能，并开源资源促进未来研究。

中文摘要：大型语言模型日益被期望处理复杂、长周期的现实世界任务，这些任务的上下文需求可能无限增长，但模型上下文窗口本质上是有限的。最近的研究探索了一种范式，其中主代理分解任务并将子任务分派给子代理，子代理执行并仅返回汇总结果，从而节省主代理的上下文预算。然而，要做好这一点需要委托智能：分解复杂任务、决定何时委托以及委托什么，并将返回的结果整合到持续的工作流程中的能力。这种能力的训练数据在自然文本中很少见，据我们所知，如何合成此类数据并训练模型获得这种能力在开源社区中基本上未被探索。为了填补这一空白，我们提出了一项初步探索，针对深度研究这一代表性长周期代理任务。具体来说，我们设计了一个引导框架，引导模型进行高质量的任务分解和委托，同时约束子代理正确返回结果以支持主代理的工作流程。引导框架生成的轨迹自然地编码了正确的委托决策，我们将其用作监督微调数据，将委托智能内化到模型权重中。我们的最终模型SearchSwarm-30B-A3B在BrowseComp上达到68.1，在BrowseComp-ZH上达到73.3，在所有同等规模的模型中取得了最佳结果。我们将发布我们的引导框架、模型权重和训练数据，以促进未来的研究。

Original abstract: Large language models are increasingly expected to handle complex, long-horizon real-world tasks whose context demands can grow without bound, yet model context windows remain inherently finite. Recent work explores a paradigm where a main agent decomposes tasks and dispatches subtasks to subagents, which execute and return only summarized results, conserving the main agent's context budget. However, performing this well requires delegation intelligence: the ability to decompose complex tasks, determine when and what to delegate, and integrate returned results into the ongoing workflow. Training data for this capability is scarce in naturally occurring text, and to our knowledge, how to synthesize such data and train models to acquire this capability remains largely unexplored in the open-source community. To bridge this gap, we present a preliminary exploration targeting deep research, a representative long-horizon agent task. Specifically, we design a harness that guides the model toward high-quality task decomposition and delegation, while constraining subagents to return results properly to support the main agent's workflow. The harness-guided trajectories naturally encode correct delegation decisions, which we use as supervised fine-tuning data to internalize delegation intelligence into model weights. Our resulting model, SearchSwarm-30B-A3B, achieves 68.1 on BrowseComp and 73.3 on BrowseComp-ZH, the best results among all models of comparable scale. We will release our harness, model weights, and training data to facilitate future research.

### [44] [Multi-Turn Evaluation of Deep Research Agents Under Process-Level Feedback](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09748v1)
*Rishabh Sabharwal,Hongru Wang,Amos Storkey,Jeff Z. Pan*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多轮评估深度研究agent在过程级反馈下改进，涉及agent评测与自我反思

TL;DR: 深度研究代理在多轮评估中，自我反思改进微小，而单次过程级反馈显著提升，但多轮收益不累积。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准仅评估单次输出，忽略了反馈指导下多轮改进的能力。

Method: 提出研究差距推理（RGI）方法，通过分析评分标准模式推断研究过程差距，并在自我反思和过程级反馈两种设置下进行多轮评估。

Result: 自我反思下净改进可忽略；单轮过程级反馈提升8-15分，纳入率35-40%；后续轮次收益不累积，智能体回归多达24%的先前满足标准。

Conclusion: 即使有针对性指导，当前深度研究代理架构仍无法实现可靠的多轮改进。

中文摘要：对于现有的深度研究代理基准测试仅评估单次输出，忽略了一个关键问题：在反馈指导下，深度研究代理能否改进其报告？为探究此问题，我们在两种反馈设置下对深度研究代理进行了多轮评估：自我反思（智能体在没有外部诊断信号的情况下修订报告）和过程级反馈（智能体接收针对其研究策略缺口的指导）。为实现过程级反馈，我们设计了研究差距推理（RGI），该方法通过分析已满足和未满足的评分标准模式来推断研究过程差距。我们的分析揭示了三个关键发现：（i）在自我反思下，智能体以几乎相等的速率纳入和回归评分标准，导致净改进可忽略不计；（ii）单轮过程级反馈带来了显著收益，将归一化分数提升约8-15分，并实现约35-40%的纳入率；（iii）这些收益在后续轮次中并不累积，智能体在重写完整报告以解决剩余差距时回归了多达24%的先前已满足标准。即使有针对性指导，我们所评估的深度研究代理架构仍无法实现可靠的多轮改进。我们的代码和结果公开于https://github.com/sabharwalrishabh/Multi-Turn-Evaluation-of-DRAs。

Original abstract: Existing benchmarks for deep research agents (DRAs) assess only single-shot outputs, ignoring a key question: can DRAs improve their reports when guided by feedback? To investigate this, we conduct a multi-turn evaluation of DRAs under two feedback settings: self-reflection, in which the agent revises its report without any external diagnostic signal, and process-level feedback, in which the agent receives guidance targeting gaps in its research strategy. To enable process-level feedback, we design Research Gap Inference (RGI), a method that analyzes patterns of satisfied and unsatisfied rubric criteria to infer research-process gaps. Our analysis reveals three key findings: (i) under self-reflection, agents incorporate and regress on rubric criteria at nearly equal rates, yielding negligible net improvement; (ii) a single round of process-level feedback yields substantial gains, raising the normalized score by approximately $8$-$15$ points and yielding a roughly $35$-$40\%$ incorporation rate; (iii) these gains do not compound over subsequent turns, as agents regress on up to $24\%$ of previously satisfied criteria when rewriting the full report to address remaining gaps. Even with targeted guidance, reliable multi-turn improvement remains out of reach for the DRA architectures we evaluate. Our code and results are publicly available at https://github.com/sabharwalrishabh/Multi-Turn-Evaluation-of-DRAs.

</details>


### [45] [Collaborative Human-Agent Protocol (CHAP)](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09751v2)
*Arsalan Shahid,Gordon Suttie,Philip Black*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: CHAP人机协作协议，定义agent审计与工作流，对coding agent设计有参考价值

TL;DR: 提出了协作人机协议（CHAP），通过结构化事件、便携交接和不可否认签名，为多人类、多智能体协作提供标准化共享工作空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有协议（MCP、A2A）未定义人类与智能体共同进行可问责工作的共享工作空间，导致关键信号（如人类判断）丢失在非结构化记录中。

Method: 设计了一个核心（工作空间、参与者、任务、工件和证据日志）和可组合配置（审查、模式、路由、审议、交接、身份、签名、审计），将覆盖操作、交接和审批转化为结构化、可审计的事件。

Result: 实现了可重放、不可抵赖的协作记录，包括带差异和理由的结构化覆盖、便携式班次交接、以及带签名的审批决策。

Conclusion: CHAP 提供了完整的规范、参考实现、测试套件和示例，为多人类多智能体协作提供了标准化基础。

中文摘要：基础模型正从响应生成转向运营角色。它们跨步骤规划、调用工具、请求人工输入、与其他智能体协调，并越来越多地承担影响客户、索赔、代码、合同和临床决策的工作。生产部署不再是单个人类监督单个模型，而是跨团队、时区和信任边界的多人多智能体协作。这种协作的技术层面仍然缺乏规范。当一个智能体草拟响应并由人类在发布前编辑时，人类判断的时刻是系统中最有价值的信号。在当前的实践中，这一信号（如果有记录）仅存在于应用程序代码、聊天线程、工单评论和团队记忆之中。两个协议标准涉及了相关问题：MCP 标准化了智能体对工具和数据的访问，A2A 标准化了智能体间的互操作性，但二者均未定义人类和智能体共同进行可问责工作的共享工作空间。本文提出了 CHAP，即协作人机协议（Collaborative Human-Agent Protocol）。在 CHAP 下，原本消失在聊天线程中的覆盖操作变成了一个结构化事件，携带差异、理由和内容哈希。班次之间的交接变成了便携信封，而非置顶消息。人类对智能体草稿的批准成为不可抵赖的签名决策，可在多年后重放。该协议通过一个小的核心（工作空间、参与者、任务、工件和仅追加的证据日志）以及可组合的配置（根据部署需求添加审查、模式、路由、审议、交接、身份、签名和透明度支持的审计）来实现。规范、参考实现、一致性测试套件和实例可参见：https://github.com/BrightbeamAI/chap

Original abstract: Foundation models are moving from response generation into operational roles. They plan across steps, call tools, request human input, coordinate with other agents, and increasingly carry responsibility for work that affects customers, claims, code, contracts, and clinical decisions. Production deployments are no longer one human supervising one model. They are multi-human, multi-agent collaborations that cross teams, time zones, and trust boundaries. The technical surface for this collaboration remains weakly specified. When an agent drafts a response and a human edits it before it ships, the moment of human judgement is the most valuable signal in the system. In current practice it is recorded, if at all, in application code, chat threads, ticket comments, and tribal memory. Two protocol standards address adjacent concerns: MCP standardises agent access to tools and data, and A2A standardises agent-to-agent interoperability. Neither defines the shared workspace in which humans and agents perform accountable work together. This paper presents CHAP, the Collaborative Human-Agent Protocol. Under CHAP, the override that used to vanish into a chat thread becomes a structured event carrying a diff, a rationale, and a content hash. The handoff between shifts becomes a portable envelope rather than a pinned message. The human approval of an agent's draft becomes a non-repudiable signed decision that can be replayed years later. The protocol achieves this through a small Core (workspaces, participants, tasks, artefacts, and an append-only evidence log) together with composable profiles that add review, modes, routing, deliberation, handoff, identity, signatures, and transparency-backed audit as deployments require them. Specification, reference implementation, conformance suite, and worked examples are available at: https://github.com/BrightbeamAI/chap

</details>


### [46] [Auto-Configuring Scientific Simulators with Lightweight Coding-Agent Adapters](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09774v2)
*Matthew Ho,Brian Liu,Jixuan Chen,Audrey Wang,Lianhui Qin*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 使用coding agent适配器自动配置科学模拟器，直接涉及agent用于自动配置与代码优化

TL;DR: 利用编码代理适配器SIGA，通过检索、程序记忆、验证和门控终止，提升科学模拟器配置的可靠性，显著减少时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 配置科学模拟器的输入文件耗时且易错，是模拟瓶颈。

Method: 提出SIGA适配器，围绕现成编码代理，提供可执行契约，包括检索、程序记忆、验证和门控终止，支持适配器自我进化。

Result: 在GEOS上提升TreeSim可靠性，从0.720到0.789，标准差降低16倍；人类校准五分钟达到专家三小时；可移植到OpenFOAM和LAMMPS。

Conclusion: SIGA有效减少配置瓶颈，通过轻量级适配器而非定制代理，且支持自我进化。

中文摘要：配置一个先进的科学模拟器，将建模目标转化为有效、可运行的输入文件，是一个持续的瓶颈，耗费领域科学家数小时到数天。输入文件是可执行接口：模拟器特定的词汇、跨文件引用、模式约束和验证规则必须对齐，模拟才能运行。我们展示这个瓶颈可以通过围绕现成的编码代理构建一个轻量级适配器来大幅减少，而不是定制化的模拟器代理。编码代理已经能导航文件、编辑代码、运行命令和修复输出；它们缺少的是模拟器的可执行契约，而重建代理循环有风险丢弃经过校准的工具使用和自我修正行为。我们引入SIGA，一个编码代理适配器，通过检索、程序记忆、代理可调用的验证和验证门控终止来提供这个契约，同时保持模型和循环冻结。因为这个契约很小且外部化，SIGA还支持适配器自我进化：先前的轨迹可以重写适配器内容，而不修改底层代理。在GEOS（一个多物理场地下模拟器）上，SIGA的主要增益是可靠性：在更难的保留任务上，它将TreeSim从0.720提升到0.789，并将跨运行标准差降低约16倍，通过防止空或无效的输入文件。在人工校准中，SIGA在大约五分钟内达到了领域专家大约三小时达到的输入文件质量。转移到OpenFOAM和LAMMPS表明该配方是可移植的但依赖于接口：当结构完整性是瓶颈时，完成门控有帮助；当值正确性是瓶颈时，记忆和检索有帮助。

Original abstract: Configuring an advanced scientific simulator, translating a modeling goal into a valid, runnable input deck, is a persistent bottleneck that costs domain scientists hours to days. Input decks are executable interfaces: simulator-specific vocabulary, cross-file references, schema constraints, and validation rules must align before a simulation can run. We show that this bottleneck can be substantially reduced with a lightweight adapter around an off-the-shelf coding agent, rather than a bespoke simulator agent. Coding agents already navigate files, edit code, run commands, and repair outputs; what they lack is the simulator's executable contract, and rebuilding the agent loop risks discarding harness-calibrated tool-use and self-correction behavior. We introduce SIGA, a coding-agent adapter that supplies this contract through retrieval, procedural memory, agent-callable validation, and validation-gated termination while leaving the model and loop frozen. Because this contract is small and external, SIGA also supports adapter self-evolution: prior trajectories can rewrite the adapter contents without modifying the underlying agent. On GEOS, a multiphysics subsurface simulator, SIGA's main gain is reliability: on harder held-out tasks it improves TreeSim from 0.720 to 0.789 and reduces across-run standard deviation by about 16x by preventing empty or invalid decks. In a human calibration, SIGA reaches in about five minutes the deck quality a domain expert reached in about three hours. Transfers to OpenFOAM and LAMMPS show the recipe is portable but interface-dependent: completion gates help when structural completeness is the bottleneck, while memory and retrieval help when value correctness is.

</details>


### [47] [Deployment-Time Memorization in Foundation-Model Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10062v2)
*Lei,Chen,Guilin Zhang,Kai Zhao,Dalmo Cirne,Andy Olsen,Xu Chu,Zeke Miller,Alet Blanken,Amine Anoun,Jerry Ting*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究agent长期记忆的隐私-效用平衡，通用agent记忆机制有启发。

TL;DR: 本文研究代理记忆设计选择（摘要攻击性、检索广度、删除模式）对个性化召回、对抗性提取和删除保真度的联合影响，发现摘要能大幅降低提取风险但引入删除残留，需全管道清除才能彻底删除。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工作未系统描述记忆设计选择如何共同影响个性化效用、提取风险和删除保真度，本研究旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 在LongMemEval数据集上，通过扫描摘要攻击性、检索广度(k)和删除模式三个设计旋钮，测量个性化召回(PR)、对抗性提取率(AER)和遗忘残留分数(FRS)，分析记忆设计的隐私-效用前沿。

Result: 关键事实摘要分别将Gemma 3 12B和GPT-4o-mini的金丝雀提取减少76%和64%，几乎不损失个性化召回；但增加k无法恢复已压缩内容的泄漏；仅原始删除导致约20%的实例中派生摘要副本可恢复，只有全管道清除或墓碑编辑才能将最差层级残留降至零。

Conclusion: 持久代理记忆必须作为一级记忆机制评估，需综合考虑其帮助代理回忆、易被提取以及可真正擦除的能力。

中文摘要：基础模型代理正日益成为长期运行的系统，它们能在交互间记住用户，使得记忆成为部署时的显式功能，而不仅仅是模型权重的属性。现有工作关注参数化记忆或审计固定记忆配置，但并未描述记忆设计选择如何共同塑造个性化效用、提取风险和删除保真度。我们将此研究表面定义为部署时记忆，将代理记忆形式化为一个隐私-效用前沿，通过个性化召回（PR）和对抗性提取率（AER）来衡量，并扫描三个记忆设计旋钮：摘要攻击性、检索广度（k）和删除模式。我们进一步引入了遗忘残留分数（FRS），以量化已删除信息是否仍能从派生记忆层级中恢复。在LongMemEval上，关键事实摘要将Gemma 3 12B的金丝雀提取减少76%，GPT-4o-mini减少64%，同时几乎保留所有个性化召回；关键是，一旦内容被压缩，增加k不再恢复泄漏。然而，相同的压缩导致了删除保真度失败：仅原始删除使得派生的摘要副本在大约20%的实例中可恢复，只有全管道清除或墓碑编辑才能将最差层级的残留降至零。总之，这些结果确立了持久代理记忆必须作为一级记忆机制进行评估——通过它帮助代理回忆的内容、它使得可提取的内容以及它能真正擦除的内容来评估。

Original abstract: Foundation-model agents are increasingly long-lived systems that remember users across interactions, making memorization an explicit deployment-time function rather than solely a property of model weights. Existing work addresses parametric memorization or audits fixed memory configurations, but does not characterize how memory-design choices jointly shape personalization utility, extraction risk, and deletion fidelity. We study this surface as deployment-time memorization, formulating agent memory as a privacy-utility frontier measured by Personalization Recall (PR) and Adversarial Extraction Rate (AER), and sweeping three memory-design knobs: summarization aggressiveness, retrieval breadth (k), and deletion mode. We further introduce the Forgetting Residue Score (FRS) to quantify whether deleted information remains recoverable from derived memory tiers. On LongMemEval, key-fact summarization reduces canary extraction by 76% on Gemma 3 12B and 64% on GPT-4o-mini while preserving nearly all personalization recall; critically, once content is compressed away, increasing k no longer restores leakage. The same compression, however, induces a deletion-fidelity failure: raw-only deletion leaves derived summary copies recoverable in approximately 20% of instances, and only full-pipeline purge or tombstone redaction drives worst-tier residue to zero. Together, these results establish that persistent agent memory must be evaluated as a first-class memorization mechanism -- assessed by what it helps agents recall, what it makes extractable, and what it can truly erase.

</details>


### [48] [Less Context, Better Agents: Efficient Context Engineering for Long-Horizon Tool-Using LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10209v1)
*Abhilasha Lodha,Mahsa Pahlavikhah Varnosfaderani,Abir Chakraborty,Abhinav Mithal*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 修剪上下文并添加摘要可以显著提升企业工具使用工作流中语言代理的可靠性和效率，最佳配置达到91.6%完整费用明细化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型作为企业工作流代理时，工具响应过长会导致上下文溢出、状态错误和高推理成本，需要优化上下文管理。

Method: 在Microsoft Dynamics 365 Finance and Operations中对GPT-5进行四种上下文配置（无用户模型、完整历史、最后5次调用、最后5次调用加摘要）的比较实验，使用50任务酒店费用基准。

Result: 无用户模型基线8.0%完成率；完整历史71.0%但高消耗；修剪到5次调用79.0%；添加摘要达到91.6%完成率和99.64%金额明细化，同时减少令牌和运行时间。

Conclusion: 对于企业工具使用工作流，选择性保留最近工具交互加紧凑摘要比保留完整历史更可靠高效，建议在类似场景中采用此策略。

中文摘要：作为企业工作流自主代理部署的大型语言模型面临一个关键挑战：来自企业系统的冗长工具响应可能导致上下文溢出、陈旧状态错误和高推理成本。我们在Microsoft Dynamics 365 Finance and Operations中使用模型上下文协议工具研究自动费用明细化问题。我们在一个50任务酒店费用基准上评估了四种GPT-5配置：无用户模型、完整对话历史、上下文修剪到最后5个工具调用/响应对、以及带自动摘要的修剪。结果取5次独立运行的平均值，用户模型在上下文工程比较中保持不变。无用户模型基线仅实现8.0%的完整明细化。完整上下文保留将完成率提高到71.0%，但消耗1,480,996个令牌和14.56小时。修剪到最后5次工具调用将完成率提高到79.0%，令牌使用减少到535,274，运行时间5.39小时。添加摘要实现最佳结果：91.6%完整明细化和99.64%平均明细化金额，使用553,374个令牌和5.79小时。我们进一步报告置信区间、效应量分析、修剪和摘要窗口的敏感性、失败分析、五种费用类型（分为三类）的结果以及使用Claude Sonnet 4.5的跨模型证据。这些结果表明，对于这类企业工具使用工作流，选择性保留最近工具交互加上紧凑摘要与完整历史保留相比可以提高可靠性和效率。

Original abstract: Large language models deployed as autonomous agents for enterprise workflows face a key challenge: verbose tool responses from enterprise systems can cause context overflow, stale-state errors, and high inference cost. We study this problem in automated expense itemization in Microsoft Dynamics 365 Finance and Operations using Model Context Protocol tools. We evaluate four GPT-5 configurations on a 50-task hotel expense benchmark: no user model, full conversation history, context pruned to the last 5 tool call/response pairs, and pruning with automated summarization. Results are averaged across 5 independent runs, with the user model held constant for the context-engineering comparison. The no-user-model baseline achieves only 8.0% complete itemization. Full-context retention improves completion to 71.0%, but consumes 1,480,996 tokens and 14.56 hours per benchmark. Pruning to the last 5 tool calls improves completion to 79.0% while reducing token use to 535,274 and runtime to 5.39 hours. Adding summarization achieves the best result: 91.6% complete itemization and 99.64% average amount itemized, with 553,374 tokens and 5.79 hours. We further report confidence intervals, effect-size analysis, sensitivity over pruning and summary windows, failure analysis, results across five expense types grouped into three categories, and cross-model evidence with Claude Sonnet 4.5. These results show that, for this class of enterprise tool-use workflow, selective retention of recent tool interactions plus compact summarization can improve both reliability and efficiency compared with full-history retention.

</details>


### [49] [Regimes: An Auditable, Held-Out-Gated Improvement Loop Demonstrated on LongMemEval with ActiveGraph](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10241v1)
*Yohei Nakajima*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 直接相关：事件溯源agent自动改进循环，含失败诊断、修复提案、验证门控，与SemOpt的自动优化高度一致。

TL;DR: 提出基于事件溯源的智能体运行时ActiveGraph，使受控改进循环可审计且可复现，并通过Regimes循环在LongMemEval-S上实现提示修复，提升准确率+0.05~+0.10。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自主改进循环因过程外部化、失败不记录、诊断不可重放、决策不透明而难以信任。

Method: 采用事件溯源架构，智能体状态为事件日志投影；设计Regimes循环，通过静态检查、沙箱执行、样本评估和保留验证实现受控改进。

Result: 在LongMemEval-S的五个保留拆分上，Regimes发现的提示修复使准确率在四个拆分提升+0.05~+0.10，一个拆分提升+0.01，其中两个拆分统计显著。

Conclusion: ActiveGraph提供可审计基础设施使受控改进循环可行；贡献包括事件溯源运行时、保留门控循环、失败机制分类法和提示即发现探针假设。

中文摘要：自主改进循环难以被信任，因为改进过程通常是附加在智能体上的外部脚手架：失败未被记录，诊断无法重放，提升或舍弃的决定被存放在侧边数据库中而非智能体自身的历史中。我们证明，事件溯源智能体运行时消除了这种摩擦，并将受控改进转变为第一类工作流。当智能体的状态是仅追加事件日志的确定性投影时，失败被记录，一次运行可以精确地从其日志重放，候选补丁限定于类型化的流水线接缝，门控是可审计的，并且每次提升或舍弃本身就是一个事件。我们通过Regimes来演示这一点，它是ActiveGraph运行时上的一个循环，该循环诊断失败的评估，在流水线点提出修复，并在静态检查、沙箱执行、样本内评估和保留验证之后才提升该修复。该循环是目标无关的：相同的控制流通过通用接口针对不同任务运行。在LongMemEval-S上，主要的失败不是检索而是调和：证据已经在组装好的上下文中，但读者回答错误。在五个带种子的保留拆分中，Regimes发现读者提示修复，使得最终保留准确率在四个拆分中提高+0.05至+0.10，在一个过度提升的拆分中提高+0.01；其中两个拆分单独显著（种子5未针对其顺序提升结构进行调整），合并计数仅为描述性，因为拆分共享一个500问题的池。持久的贡献包括：ActiveGraph作为可审计的基础设施使得受控改进循环可行，它所支持的保留门控循环，将每个失败路由到流水线位置的失败机制分类法（其相对于无路由基线的边际价值是主要的开放问题），以及提示即发现探针的假设。

Original abstract: Autonomous improvement loops are hard to trust because the improvement process is usually external scaffolding bolted onto the agent: failures go unlogged, diagnoses cannot be replayed, and promote-or-discard decisions land in a side database rather than the agent's own history. We show that an event-sourced agent runtime removes that friction and turns controlled improvement into a first-class workflow. When the agent's state is a deterministic projection of an append-only event log, failures are recorded, a run replays exactly from its log, candidate patches scope to typed pipeline seams, gates are auditable, and every promotion or discard is itself an event. We demonstrate this with Regimes, a loop on the ActiveGraph runtime that diagnoses failed evaluations, proposes a repair at a pipeline point, and promotes it only after static checks, sandbox execution, in-sample evaluation, and held-out validation. The loop is target-agnostic: the same control flow runs against different tasks through a common interface. On LongMemEval-S the dominant failure is not retrieval but reconciliation: the evidence is already in the assembled context, yet the reader answers incorrectly. Across five seeded held-out splits, Regimes discovers reader-prompt repairs that improve final held-out accuracy by +0.05 to +0.10 in four splits and +0.01 in one over-promotion split; two splits are individually significant (seed 5 unadjusted for its sequential promotion structure), and the pooled count is descriptive only, since the splits share one 500-question pool. The durable contributions are ActiveGraph as an auditable substrate that makes controlled improvement loops tractable, the held-out-gated loop it supports, the failure-regime taxonomy routing each failure to a pipeline location (whose marginal value over an unrouted baseline is the primary open question), and the prompt-as-discovery-probe hypothesis.

</details>

### [50] [FMplex: Model Virtualization for Serving Extensible Foundation Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09643v1)
*Hetvi Shastri,Pragya Sharma,Walid A. Hanafy,David Irwin,Mani Srivastava,Prashant Shenoy*

Main category: cs.DC

Selection reason: 模型虚拟化服务系统，批处理调度可借鉴于agent部署优化

TL;DR: FMplex是一个通过共享基础模型骨干网络来服务多个下游任务的系统，使用虚拟基础模型抽象和批量感知调度，显著降低延迟并提高任务密度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模型服务系统为每个任务部署独立模型实例，导致骨干网络重复、加速器内存浪费、批处理和加载成本无法摊销。

Method: 提出FMplex，将FM骨干作为虚拟化基板，为每个任务提供虚拟基础模型（vFM）抽象，实现共享物理FM的同时保留任务扩展和隔离；并设计批量感知公平队列调度器，结合加权任务共享和跨任务批处理。

Result: 在7个FM骨干（16变体）和92个任务上，延迟比空间分区降低80%，比尽力共置降低33.3%，集群规模下托管任务数增加6倍。

Conclusion: FMplex通过共享骨干网络和智能调度，有效提升模型服务系统的效率和可扩展性，适用于多任务场景。

中文摘要：基础模型（FMs）越来越多地被用作语言、视觉、时间序列和多模态应用中下游任务的骨干网络。然而，现有的模型服务系统将每个定制任务部署为一个独立的模型实例，从而复制了重型骨干网络，浪费了加速器内存，并失去了摊销批处理和加载成本的机会。本文提出了FMplex，一个将FM骨干网络视为虚拟化基板以进行部署共享的服务系统。FMplex为每个任务提供一个虚拟基础模型（vFM），即一个由共享物理FM支持的逻辑私有的FM实例。这种抽象允许独立定制的任务共享一个骨干网络，同时保留任务特定的扩展、独立生命周期和任务级隔离。此外，我们提出了一个批量感知的公平队列调度器，该调度器结合了加权任务级共享以及跨共置任务的批内和批间处理。我们实现了一个基于FMplex的服务栈，涵盖任务构建、共享感知部署和运行时执行。在7个FM骨干网络（16个变体）和92个下游任务上，与空间分区相比，FMplex将延迟降低了高达80%，与尽力而为的共置相比降低了33.3%，同时在集群规模上托管的任务数量最多可增加6倍。

Original abstract: Foundation models (FMs) are increasingly used as backbones for downstream tasks across language, vision, time-series, and multimodal applications. Yet existing model-serving systems deploy each customized task as an independent model instance, thereby replicating heavyweight backbones, wasting accelerator memory, and losing opportunities to amortize batching and loading costs. This paper presents FMplex, a serving system that treats FM backbones as a virtualization substrate for deployment sharing. FMplex presents each task with a virtual foundation model (vFM), a logically private FM instance backed by a shared physical FM. This abstraction lets independently customized tasks share a backbone while preserving task-specific extensions, independent lifecycles, and task-level isolation. In addition, we propose a batch-aware fair-queueing scheduler that combines weighted task-level sharing with inter- and intra-task batching across colocated tasks. We implement a FMplex-based serving stack spanning task construction, sharing-aware deployment, and runtime execution. Across 7 FM backbones (16 variants) and 92 downstream tasks, FMplex reduces latency by up to 80% over spatial partitioning and 33.3% over best-effort co-location, while hosting up to 6x more tasks at cluster scale.

</details>

### [51] [Cheap Reward Hacking Detection](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08893v1)
*Iván Belenky,Joaquín Itria,Steven Johns*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出检测reward hacking的方法，直接涉及agent安全与可靠性。

TL;DR: 使用小Transformer编码器将轨迹映射到球面，线性探针检测奖励黑客，性能优于LLM评判且成本降低四个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 奖励黑客检测通常依赖高成本的LLM评判，本文旨在通过更廉价的嵌入方法实现类似或更优的检测性能。

Method: 训练小型Transformer编码器，将Terminal-Wrench轨迹嵌入单位球面，使嵌入距离近似奖励和元数据信号的L1距离；然后在嵌入上训练线性探针进行二分类检测。

Result: 在清洗测试集上AUC为0.9467，TPR@5%FPR为0.8296；与LLM评判相比，AUC相近但TPR更高，且每条轨迹成本低约四个数量级；去除自然语言推理后AUC降至0.6213。

Conclusion: 该方法以极低成本实现了与LLM评判相当的奖励黑客检测性能，但依赖于自然语言推理特征，并非纯行为分析。

中文摘要：一个小型Transformer编码器被训练用于将Terminal-Wrench轨迹映射到一个单位球面上，其中嵌入距离近似于奖励和元数据信号之间的L1距离。在该嵌入之上使用线性探针，在清洗后的测试集上检测奖励黑客攻击，AUC为0.9467，5%假阳性率下的真阳性率为0.8296，与基于TW消毒的LLM作为评判的AUC（清洗后的分割上为0.9510）相当，并且在相同信息条件下，在5%假阳性率下的真阳性率（0.7130 vs 0.8296）上超过它，而每条轨迹的成本大约低四个数量级。该编码器不是纯粹的行为读取器：在探针时从其输入中去除自然语言推理，AUC降至0.6213。

Original abstract: A small transformer encoder is trained to map Terminal-Wrench trajectories onto a unit sphere where embedding distance approximates the $L_1$ distance between reward and metadata signals. A linear probe on top of that embedding detects reward hacking on the cleaned test split with AUC $0.9467$ and TPR@5%FPR $0.8296$, matching the TW sanitized LLM-as-judge AUC ($0.9510$ on the cleaned split) and exceeding its TPR@5%FPR ($0.7130$ vs $0.8296$) on the same information condition, at roughly four orders of magnitude lower per-trajectory cost. The encoder is not a pure behavior reader: stripping natural-language reasoning from its input at probe time drops AUC to $0.6213$.

</details>


### [52] [INFUSER: Influence-Guided Self-Evolution Improves Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09052v3)
*Siyu Chen,Miao Lu,Beining Wu,Heejune Sheen,Fengzhuo Zhang,Shuangning Li,Zhiyuan Li,Jose Blanchet,Tianhao Wang,Zhuoran Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 自我进化框架（Generator-Solver co-training），可迁移至代码优化agent的自主改进

TL;DR: 提出INFUSER框架，通过生成器与求解器协同进化，利用影响分数和DuGRPO算法实现自适应课程学习，显著提升模型推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自进化方法依赖精心策划数据或无效的难度启发式，无法有效提升求解器性能。

Method: 提出INFUSER，包含生成器和求解器的迭代协同训练框架，生成器通过DuGRPO优化影响分数产生有用问题，求解器通过标准正确性奖励学习。

Result: 在Qwen3-8B-Base上，Olympiad和SuperGPQA基准相对提升超20%，8B生成器优于32B冻结生成器。

Conclusion: INFUSER通过自适应课程和学习信号优化，有效提升自进化推理能力，且具灵活性和泛化性。

中文摘要：自我进化为更强的推理提供了一条可扩展的路径：预训练语言模型在仅需极少外部监督的情况下自我改进。然而，现有方法要么依赖于精心策划或教师生成的训练数据，要么当生成器无监督运行时，通过一个不一定能改进求解器的难度启发式来奖励它。我们引入了INFUSER，一个具有两个共同演化角色的迭代协同训练框架：一个生成器，从自动收集的非结构化文档池中草拟问题和参考答案；以及一个求解器，通过在其上训练来改进。求解器使用标准正确性奖励（以生成器提供的答案为基准）进行训练，而生成器则通过一个优化器感知的影响分数来奖励，该分数衡量每个提出的问题是否真的能改进求解器在目标分布上的表现。由于这种连续、嘈杂的影响分数不适合标准的GRPO，我们提出了DuGRPO，一种GRPO的双归一化变体，用于生成器训练。这些结合起来将文档池转化为一个自适应课程，优先考虑对当前求解器有用的问题，而不仅仅是困难的问题。在Qwen3-8B-Base上，INFUSER在Olympiad和SuperGPQA基准测试中相比强自进化基线实现了超过20%的相对改进，并且一个8B的INFUSER共同演化生成器在数学和编程任务上的表现优于冻结的32B思考生成器。消融实验证实了每个设计选择的必要性，而两个扩展——将INFUSER应用于指令微调锚点并辅以规则可验证的RLVR数据——进一步展示了框架的灵活性和泛化性。代码可在https://github.com/FFishy-git/INFUSER获取。

Original abstract: Self-evolution offers a scalable path to stronger reasoning: a pretrained language model improves itself with only minimal external supervision. Yet existing methods either depend on extensively curated or teacher-generated training data, or, when the generator runs unsupervised, reward it by a difficulty heuristic that need not improve the solver. We introduce INFUSER, an iterative co-training framework with two co-evolving roles: a Generator that drafts questions and reference golden answers from a pool of unstructured, automatically collected documents, and a Solver that improves by training on them. The solver is trained with standard correctness rewards against the generator-provided answers, while the generator is rewarded by an optimizer-aware influence score that measures whether each proposed question would actually improve the solver on the target distribution. Because this continuous, noisy influence score is poorly served by standard GRPO, we propose DuGRPO, a dual-normalized variant of GRPO, for generator training. Together, these turn the document pool into an adaptive curriculum that favors questions useful to the current solver, not just hard ones. On Qwen3-8B-Base, INFUSER outperforms strong self-evolution baselines with over 20% relative improvement on Olympiad and SuperGPQA benchmarks, and an 8B INFUSER co-evolving generator outperforms a frozen 32B thinking generator on math and coding. Ablations confirm each design choice is necessary, and two extensions, applying INFUSER to an instruction-finetuned anchor and augmenting it with rule-verifiable RLVR data, further demonstrate the flexibility and generalizability of the framework. Code is available at https://github.com/FFishy-git/INFUSER.

</details>


### [53] [Internalizing Geometric Law: Learning from Solver Residuals for Precision-Critical Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09278v1)
*Rafael Cabral,Pang Zixi,Ziyi Shou,Shen Xin*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出Saturating Additive Rewards奖励设计，可迁移至agent多约束任务

TL;DR: 提出PyGeoX和PyGeoX-Bench，发现离群梯度掩蔽问题，并提出饱和加法奖励（SAR）以在几何约束合成任务中显著提升求解率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在精度关键领域（如技术图表和机械设计）中常因输出需满足严格几何约束而产生幻觉，现有开放几何综合方法难以处理大量相互作用约束。

Method: 设计可编程几何DSL PyGeoX，将声明性约束编译为可微损失；构建分层基准PyGeoX-Bench；提出饱和加法奖励（SAR），将奖励分解为有界的每约束项，以缓解离群梯度掩蔽问题。

Result: 与MSE奖励相比，SAR将硬档求解率提升2.3倍，8B模型在基准上与更大前沿系统竞争力相当。

Conclusion: 通过SAR和PyGeoX框架，有效增强了语言模型在几何约束任务上的性能，并提供可复现的基准和工具，推动了该领域的发展。

中文摘要：大型语言模型在精度要求极高的领域（如技术图表绘制和机械设计）中经常出现幻觉，在这些领域中输出必须满足严格的几何约束。我们研究从自然语言进行开放式几何综合：将自由形式的描述转化为精确的构造，其实体必须同时满足数十个相互作用的约束。为了使这一问题可处理，我们发布了PyGeoX，一个可编程的几何特定领域语言，它将声明性约束编译成可微损失函数，以及PyGeoX-Bench，一个包含300个问题的分层套件，每个约束都有可验证的奖励。使用PyGeoX作为验证器，我们识别出一种我们称之为离群梯度掩蔽的失败模式：在全范数奖励（任何通过单一范数聚合残差的方案，例如exp(-MSE)）下，单个离群约束可以抵消所有其他约束的学习信号。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了饱和加法奖励（SAR），它将奖励分解为有界的每约束项，保留部分进展并确保即使在严重违反约束的情况下也能保持一致的梯度。与基于MSE的奖励（几何求解器的自然基线）相比，SAR将硬档求解率提高了2.3倍，并且由此得到的8B模型在此基准上与更大的前沿系统具有竞争力。我们在https://github.com/Huawei-AI4Math/PyGeoX上发布了引擎、基准和数据。

Original abstract: Large Language Models frequently hallucinate in precision-critical domains such as technical diagramming and mechanical design, where outputs must satisfy strict geometric constraints. We study open-ended geometric synthesis from natural language: translating free-form descriptions into precise constructions whose entities must simultaneously satisfy dozens of interacting constraints. To make this tractable, we release PyGeoX, a programmable geometric DSL that compiles declarative constraints into a differentiable loss, and PyGeoX-Bench, a stratified suite of 300 problems with per-constraint verifiable rewards. Using PyGeoX as a verifier, we identify a failure mode we call Outlier Gradient Masking: under global-norm rewards (any scheme that aggregates residuals through a single norm, for example, $\exp(-\mathrm{MSE})$), a single outlier constraint can nullify the learning signal across all others. To address this, we propose Saturating Additive Rewards (SAR), which decompose the reward into bounded per-constraint terms, preserving partial progress and ensuring consistent gradients even under severe violations. Against MSE-based rewards, the natural baseline for geometry solvers, SAR improves the hard-tier solving rate by $2.3\times$, and the resulting 8B model is competitive with much larger frontier systems on this benchmark. We release the engine, benchmark, and data at https://github.com/Huawei-AI4Math/PyGeoX.

### [54] [Reasoning Arena: Trace Tournaments When Verifiable Rewards Fall Short](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09380v1)
*Han Zhou,Adam X. Yang,Laurence Aitchison,Anna Korhonen,Albert Q. Jiang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 推理RL训练中处理无梯度组，可迁移至agent奖励设计

TL;DR: 提出Reasoning Arena框架，通过轨迹锦标赛和Bradley-Terry模型将无信息奖励转化为有用信号，提升推理性能并加速训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLVR方法在组级奖励无差异时缺乏梯度信号，浪费样本，需利用这些样本的推理质量信息。

Method: 构建轨迹锦标赛，对推理轨迹进行成对比较；使用动态锚点池高效建立相对排名，并在不完全比较图上拟合Bradley-Terry模型以生成相对奖励信号。

Result: 在竞赛数学和编码基准上平均提升7.6%，训练加速27%-41%，节省近50%生成计算。

Conclusion: Reasoning Arena有效利用零优势样本，提升推理性能并显著加速训练。

中文摘要：具有可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已成为通过基于结果的监督来提高大型语言模型推理能力的主要范式。然而，可验证奖励在组级别经常变得无信息：当给定提示的所有采样轨迹获得相同奖励时，组相对优势估计不提供梯度信号，尽管这些轨迹在推理质量上可能有很大差异。我们提出Reasoning Arena，一种自适应训练框架，将这种非多样性的奖励组路由到裁判系统，而不是丢弃它们。除了检查最终答案，Reasoning Arena构建轨迹锦标赛，其中推理轨迹被逐对比较以揭示组内更细粒度的偏好，将推理质量转化为丰富的相对奖励信号。为了使奖励估计高效，而不是穷举比较每一对，每个新轨迹与一个小的、动态更新的先前生成轨迹池作为锚点进行评估，以有效建立相对排名。然后我们在不完全比较图上拟合Bradley-Terry模型，实现无需二次成对比较的可扩展强化学习集成。实证结果表明，Reasoning Arena在竞赛数学和编码基准上平均比RLVR基线高7.6%。通过将原本浪费的零优势样本转化为有用的梯度更新，我们的方法将训练加速27%至41%，节省近50%的生成计算，并显著提高整体推理性能。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has become a leading paradigm for improving the reasoning ability of large language models through outcome-based supervision. However, verifiable rewards frequently become uninformative at the group level: when all sampled traces of a given prompt receive identical rewards, group-relative advantage estimation provides no gradient signal, even though the traces may differ substantially in reasoning quality. We propose Reasoning Arena, an adaptive training framework that routes such non-diverse reward groups to a judge system instead of discarding them. Beyond examining the final answer, Reasoning Arena constructs trace tournaments, where reasoning traces are compared head-to-head to expose finer-grained preferences within the group, converting reasoning quality into rich relative reward signals. To make reward estimation efficient, rather than exhaustively comparing every pair, each new trace is evaluated against a small, dynamically updated pool of previously generated traces as anchors to efficiently establish a relative ranking. We then fit a Bradley-Terry model on the incomplete comparison graph, enabling scalable RL integration without quadratic pairwise comparisons. Empirical results demonstrate that Reasoning Arena consistently outperforms the RLVR baseline by 7.6% on average in competition mathematics and coding benchmarks. By converting otherwise wasted zero-advantage samples into useful gradient updates, our method accelerates training by 27% to 41%, saving nearly 50% of generation compute, and substantially improves overall reasoning performance.

</details>


### [55] [LargeMonitor: Monitoring Online Task-Free Continual Learning via Large Pretrained Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09430v1)
*Mingqi Yuan,Xiaoquan Sun,Shihao Luo,Jiayu Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 利用大模型监控持续学习中的漂移，提供检测与诊断机制，可迁移至agent自适应策略。

TL;DR: LargeMonitor利用大型预训练模型实现无任务持续学习中的零样本漂移检测与语义诊断，并能自适应部署针对性优化策略，提升现有算法性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有在线无任务持续学习算法依赖训练耦合的动态（如损失波动）来检测漂移，无法区分不同结构起源的分布漂移，导致固定策略不适用所有变化。

Method: 提出LargeMonitor框架，包含解耦的检测模块（利用冻结的大型视觉模型稳定表示实现零样本漂移检测）和上下文感知诊断模块（利用大型多模态模型解释漂移的语义病因），双阶段后自动选择优化策略。

Result: 在多个TFCL设置和基准上，LargeMonitor实现精确鲁棒的检测和诊断，并持续提升现有在线TFCL算法的性能。

Conclusion: 通过解耦检测与诊断，LargeMonitor能有效应对无任务持续学习中分布漂移的多样性，为自适应优化提供新范式。

中文摘要：在线无任务持续学习要求智能代理在严格单次遍历约束下，从无界、非平稳数据流中顺序积累知识，且没有任何显式任务标识。现有的在线无任务持续学习范式主要依赖于参数高效的提示调整或由训练耦合优化动态（如经验损失波动或潜在距离演变）驱动的动态结构扩展。因此，这些训练耦合的求解器对分布漂移的结构起源仍然不可知，机械地在根本不同的流变化上强制执行固定策略。为了解决这一差距，我们提出了LargeMonitor，一个利用大型预训练基础模型自主编排无任务持续适应的框架。具体来说，LargeMonitor引入了一个解耦的检测模块，利用大型视觉模型的冻结稳定表示空间，实现鲁棒的、零样本的漂移检测，无需训练依赖的干扰或脆弱的阈值调整。在确认漂移后，该框架激活一个由大型多模态模型驱动的上下文感知诊断模块，以解释流变化的精确语义病因（例如，新类别出现与环境领域转移）。这种双阶段能力使持续学习器能够动态部署自适应且特定于变化的优化策略。在多个无任务持续学习设置和基准上的大量实验表明，LargeMonitor能够精确、鲁棒地检测和诊断复杂数据流，同时持续提高现有在线无任务持续学习算法的性能。

Original abstract: Online task-free continual learning (TFCL) requires intelligent agents to sequentially accumulate knowledge from an unbounded, non-stationary data stream under strict single-pass constraints and without any explicit task identifiers. Existing online TFCL paradigms primarily rely on parameter-efficient prompt tuning or dynamic structure expansion driven by training-coupled optimization dynamics, such as empirical loss fluctuations or evolving latent distances. As a result, these training-coupled solvers remain agnostic to the structural origins of distribution drift, mechanically enforcing a fixed strategy across fundamentally distinct streaming variations. To address this gap, we propose LargeMonitor, a framework that leverages large pretrained foundation models to autonomously orchestrate task-free continuous adaptation. Specifically, LargeMonitor introduces a decoupled detection module utilizing the frozen, stable representation space of large vision models (LVMs) to achieve robust, zero-shot drift detection without training-dependent interference or brittle threshold tuning. Upon a confirmed drift, the framework activates a context-aware diagnostic module driven by large multimodal models (LMMs) to interpret the precise semantic etiologies of the stream variation (e.g., novel class emergence vs. environmental domain shift). This dual-stage capability empowers the continuous learner to dynamically deploy adaptive and shift-specific optimization strategies. Extensive experiments across multiple TFCL settings and benchmarks demonstrate that LargeMonitor achieves precise, robust detection and diagnosis of complex data streams while consistently improving the performance of existing online TFCL algorithms.

### [56] [3SPO: State-Score-Supervised Policy Optimization for LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09961v1)
*Yu Han,Kailing Li,Yang Jiao,Yulin Dai,Yuqian Fu,Linhai Zhuo,Tianwen Qian*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出3SPO RL算法，直接用于LLM agent策略优化，可迁移。

TL;DR: 提出3SPO算法，通过状态分数监督实现步骤级策略优化，在ALFWorld和WebShop上显著优于GRPO。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RL算法在轨迹级别优化，难以处理多轮智能体设置中的稀疏延迟奖励和步骤间信用分配问题。

Method: 提出3SPO算法，基于历史成功率计算状态分数，进行步骤级信用分配、自适应滚动和步骤后策略优化，无需值函数估计或额外模型。

Result: 在ALFWorld和WebShop上，3SPO相比GRPO分别提升22.6%和15.6分，同时实现2.4倍状态探索和1.8倍收敛加速。

Conclusion: 3SPO通过状态分数监督有效解决了多轮智能体RL中的信用分配问题，理论和实验均验证其优越性。

中文摘要：通过强化学习（RL）将大型语言模型（LLM）训练为自主智能体，已使前沿模型在长 horizon 任务中实现了超人类性能。然而，现有的RL算法在轨迹级别操作，仅在收集完整的 episode 轨迹后才进行策略优化。这种粗粒度方法在多轮智能体设置中面临根本性挑战，因为奖励稀疏、延迟，且跨单个步骤的信用分配至关重要。在这项工作中，我们提出\textbf{状态分数监督策略优化（3SPO）}，一种新颖的RL算法，通过动态状态分数监督进行步骤后策略优化。在每个步骤，3SPO基于历史成功率计算状态分数，监督步骤级信用分配、自适应滚动和步骤后策略优化，无需值函数估计或额外的辅助模型。理论上，在每个状态 bandit 抽象下，我们表明所提出的分数监督分配机制实现了对数分配遗憾，并为动作识别、分数可区分性和过滤稳定性提供了样本复杂度保证。在ALFWorld和WebShop上使用Qwen2.5-1.5B/7B-Instruct的实验表明，3SPO在ALFWorld上始终优于GRPO $+22.6\%$，在WebShop上高出$+15.6$分，同时使用相当的资源实现了$2.4\times$更多的状态探索和$1.8\times$更快的收敛。代码可在https://github.com/genalyu/3SPO获取。

Original abstract: Training large language models (LLMs) as autonomous agents via reinforcement learning (RL) has enabled frontier models to achieve superhuman performance in long-horizon tasks. However, existing RL algorithms operate at the trajectory level, performing policy optimization only after collecting complete episode rollouts. This coarse-grained approach faces fundamental challenges in multi-turn agent settings where rewards are sparse, delayed, and credit assignment across individual steps is critical. In this work, we propose \textbf{State-Score-Supervised Policy Optimization (3SPO)}, a novel RL algorithm that performs post-step policy optimization with dynamic state score supervision. At each step, 3SPO computes the state score based on historical success rates, supervising step-wise credit assignment, adaptive rollout and post-step policy optimization without requiring value function estimation or additional auxiliary models. Theoretically, under a per-state bandit abstraction, we show that the proposed score-supervised allocation mechanism achieves logarithmic allocation regret and provide sample-complexity guarantees for action identification, score distinguishability, and filtering stability. Experiments on ALFWorld and WebShop with Qwen2.5-1.5B/7B-Instruct show that 3SPO consistently outperforms GRPO by $+22.6\%$ on ALFWorld and $+15.6$ points on WebShop, while using comparable resources to achieve $2.4\times$ more state exploration and $1.8\times$ faster convergence. Code is available at https://github.com/genalyu/3SPO.

### [57] [Safe-RULE: Safe Reinforcement UnLEarning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09559v1)

Result: 在基准Safe RL任务上，该方法有效提升安全性能，抵御数据投毒攻击。

Conclusion: Safe-RULE为离线Safe RL提供了一种有效的防御机制，无需重新训练或原始环境访问。

中文摘要：离线安全强化学习（Safe RL）使得无需在线交互即可进行策略学习，适用于机器人系统等安全关键型系统。然而，其对静态数据集的依赖使得离线Safe RL容易受到数据投毒攻击，攻击者注入恶意样本，危及安全性并导致不安全的策略行为。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种新的学习范式，名为安全强化遗忘（Safe-RULE），作为一种防御框架，无需从头重新训练或访问原始训练环境即可移除中毒数据的影响。我们进一步将强化遗忘扩展到离线Safe RL，通过在遗忘过程中明确考虑任务性能和安全约束。在基准Safe RL任务上的实验表明，我们的方法有效提升了针对数据投毒攻击的安全性能。

Original abstract: Offline safe reinforcement learning (Safe RL) enables policy learning without online interactions, making it suitable for safety-critical systems such as robotics systems. However, its reliance on static datasets exposes offline Safe RL to data poisoning attacks, where adversaries inject malicious samples that compromise safety and induce unsafe policy behavior. In this work, we propose a new learning paradigm, named safe reinforcement unlearning (Safe-RULE), used as a defense framework to remove the influence of poisoned data without retraining from scratch or requiring access to the original training environment. We further extend reinforcement unlearning to offline Safe RL by explicitly accounting for both task performance and safety constraints during the unlearning process. Experiments across benchmark Safe RL tasks demonstrate that our approach effectively enhances safety performance against data poisoning attacks.

### [58] [Bittensor Agent Arenas as a Trajectory Primitive: Distilling a Shopping Agent from ShoppingBench Subnet Traces](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10064v1)
*Shardul Bansal,Seth Schilbe,Jarrod Barnes*
